Foreiga representative of a US resettlement agency which is interested in
bringing the subject of this report to the US. The following information
was forwarded to the headquarters of that agency to determine placement
possibilities in the US. To date, no decision has been reached.
NAME: Zanie Perkone
DATE AND PLACE OF BIRTH: 21 May 1888 at Zemite, Latvia
PRESSEIT ADDRESS: Eselingen-Neckar, Pfaffstrasse 1, US Zone of Germany
NATIONALITY: Latvian
MARITAL STATUS: Married (Wife and mother-in-law will temporarily not
to to the US.)
EDUCATION: Attended elementary school in Irilava, Orenci, Zemite from
1895 to 1899; attended high school in Tukuma, Latvia from
1900 to 1904; attended Poltytechnical Institute in Riga,
Latvia, from 1908 to 1914, graduated in latter year, majored
in engineering teaching.
EXPERIENCE: Chief of technical and supply department, cooperative of
the University of the Indian and U.S. Latvia from 1928 to 1937; consulting
engineer for the Baltic States "Alfria-Adstra" from 1937 to
1940; engineer and dispatcher for "Machine Bulider" Trust
in Riga, Latvia, from 1940 to June 1941; director of the
Riga Screw & Hut Works at Riga, Latvia, from 1941; director of the
Riga, Latvia, from 1941; director of the National Association
of M1lk, Zat and Esge at Hamburg, Germany, from December
1944 to August 1946; teacher of mathematics at Latvian soo-
ondary school at DP Camp Oxford Alt-Garse, Dedelstorf,
Germany, from February 1946 to August 1949; teacher at INB
vocational training center at Ludvigsburg, Germany, from
September 1949 to February 1950; deputy resettlement officer
for Luthers and Federation at Ludvigsburg, Germany,
February 1950 to present.

THIS, IS UNEVALUATED INFORMATION
SOURCE
Foreign representative of a US resettlement agency which is interested in
bringing the subject of this report to the US. The following information
was forwarded to the headquarters of that agency to determine placement
possibilities in the US. To date, no decision has been reached.
KANCE: Eduard 0 Von Roka
DATE AND PLACE OF BIRTH: 25 April 1922 in Budapest, Hungary
PRESENT ADDRESS: Göttingen, Germany
NATIONALITY: Hungarian
NARITAL STATUS: Single
EDUCATION: Graduated from yomnastum in Budapest, Hungary in 1940, with
honors. Attended Technische Hochschule in Berlin-Charlotten-
burg, Germany from 1940 to 1945, physicist.
EXPERIENCE: Experimental work in research, laboratory work, from 1943
to 1945 at the Institute of Professor Goleger: worked in
thermodynamics for Dr. Pascual Jordan, Mathematical Institute,
Göttingen, Germany, from 1945 to 1946, quoted as nuclear
physicalist. for Max Planck; Institut für Physik at Ostlingen,
Germany, From 1946 to present.
PUBLICATIONS: Las published various articles on nuclear physics; also
were popular articles on phylcise for magnasines and period-
icals.
SPECIAL HONOR: Received acholarship from Hungarian Government in 1940
to study in Germany from 1940 to 1945.
COMMENTS BY SOURCE: In two letters of recommendation forwarded by
Von Roka's last two employers, he was described
as exceptionally able and talented.

00-8-30678
- 2 -
Teacher of Natural History, Mathematics and Physics at
the Aixonndria Institute in Rowno, Poland, from 1926
to 1939.
Did laboratory work at a dairy cooperative in Janow,
Poland, from 1939 to 1944.
Was at forced labor in Germany from 1944 to 1945.
Professor, Chair of Zoology in the Uracinian Polytechnicel
Institute at Nou Ulm, Germany from 1945 to 1960.
CONNATED OF LANGUAGES: Knows Russian, Ukrainian and Polish.
SOURCE'S CONSENTS: Subject has done extensive work in field of micro-
photography.
